 co / tscgap9til The country, which is making rapid strides in the world of Internet, is currently debating the net neutrality in India
 yah mudda itnaa bada he ki telecom niamak sanstha (TRAI) ne 118 pej kaa mashwara jari karke, yugers se is sambandh main raay maangi he
 If you also want to give an opinion about this, you can give it by 24 April
 raay dene se pehle jaane net neutrality ke bare main sab kuch:kya he net neutrality?net neutrality shabd kaa pehali baar istemaal colombia uniwarsity main media lau ke professor team vu ne kiya tha
 According to the Net Neutrality principle, any service provider will give equal status to any content, data and applications of the Internet
 koi bhi website or pej tab tak nahin block kiye jaae jab tak ki us par koi gaiyr kanoonee tathy na ho
 This means that the Internet will give equal space to all the websites, big and small
 net neutrality se sambandhit mukhya baaten1
 Net neutrality is the principle that a service provider company gives equal status to all data
 2
 Whether the service is to visit the website or get other content
 3
 Due to net neutrality, the service provider company can neither block the data nor slow down its speed
 4
 In the absence of net neutrality, operators can charge money separately for calling services in addition to data prices
 5
 If net neutrality is not implemented, mobile companies may also charge more for these services separately
 net neutrality hatane par aap kyon honge pareshaan:net neutrality ko agar lagu nahin kiya gaya to iskaa sidhaa asar aapaki jebon par pad saktaa he
 You may have fewer options
 aapkoseva pradaan karne vaali companyapake bare main yah nirnay le sakati he ki aapako koun si website, news, contate kab or kitna dekhnaa he yaa nahin
 At present, you have the facility that you can access any site on the Internet at the same speed as foreign, popular, and unpopular, but when it is not there, you will not be able to access the entire site with the same speed
 sarvice prowider aapse whatsap, skip is tarah kii anya suvidhaon ke liye alag se charge le sakati hai
 Apart from this, the company can interrupt its calling service by reducing the data speed of these apps
 net neutralityke lagu na hone kaa sabase zyada asar un chote bijness maalikon or antraprenyor par ho saktaa he, jinhone apana online bijness shuru kiya he
 Currently, they directly promote and sell their products through the Internet
 bharat jaise desh ko isaki sakht jarurat he kyonki yahaan internet bijness kii shuruyaat hue kuch hi saal hue hai or is kshetra main yuvaaon ko bade paimaane par job bhi mil rahi he
 If we leave the business for a while, then it is also necessary for our freedom of speech
 net neutrality naa hone ke kaaran koi bhi contate aasaani se block kiye ja sakegaa
 Why Net companies are troubled by the Net Neutrality principle: Internet calling facility like Skype, whatsapp is affecting the business of telecom companies
 companiyon ne isse bachane ke liye data keemten badha di thim
 Last year, a mobile service provider announced a charge of up to Rs 1,000 on the use of one GB of data on voip i
e
 Voice over Internet Protocol services
 magar aalochanaon ke kaaran usne ise waapas le liya tha
 Telecom companies are now looking for such a business option where they too can earn big money from internet world
 operators chaahate hai ki jis tarah se bazaar main saare fal kaa daam ek jaisaa nahin hota
 Grape is more expensive than orange, in the same way, money should be collected according to content and data
 darasal, yah puraa maamla bazaar main apane aapako majbootee se sthapit karne kaa he or bazaar main vahi sthapit ho paaegaa jo paristhitayon ko apane anusaar dhaalega
 Due to the non-implementation of net neutrality, big companies like Google, Facebook, Reliance, Airtel, Vodafone will lose their race in small capital businesses
 bharat jaise desh main jahaan berogari sabase zyada he, vahaan internet ne yuvaaon kowebsitake madhyam se rojgaar paane or shuru karne ke kai maukey die hai
 If net neutrality is not implemented, it will also have an impact on generating employment

 tippaniyan Similarly, if the amount available in the accounts is less than 50 to 75 per cent of the minimum balance, then the bank will charge a penalty of Rs 75 and it will include service tax separately

 Strawberries - Strawberries are the best fruit for weight loss
 inamen bahut kam carb hota he or iske saath hi antioxident ke maamle main rich hoti he
 According to the US Department of Agriculture data (USDA), 100 grams of strawberries contain only 8 grams of carbohydrate
 tarbooz-vajan ghataane ke liye tarbooz bhi kargar fal he kyonki isamen bhi kam calories hoti he
 According to the USDA, 100 grams of watermelon contains only 8 grams of carbohydrates
 peach-wet los ke liye peach bhi ek acha vikalp ho saktaa he
 100 grams of peach contains only 10 grams of carbohydrate
